<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.CacheConfiguration">CacheConfiguration
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.RouteConfigurationOverrideActionParameters">RouteConfigurationOverrideActionParameters</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Caching settings for a caching-type route. To disable caching, do not provide a cacheConfiguration object.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>cacheBehavior</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.CacheConfiguration_CacheBehavior">
CacheConfiguration_CacheBehavior
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CacheBehavior: Caching behavior for the requests</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>cacheDuration</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CacheDuration: The duration for which the content needs to be cached. Allowed format is [d.]hh:mm:ss</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isCompressionEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.CacheConfiguration_IsCompressionEnabled">
CacheConfiguration_IsCompressionEnabled
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsCompressionEnabled: Indicates whether content compression is enabled. If compression is enabled, content will be
served as compressed if user requests for a compressed version. Content won&rsquo;t be compressed on AzureFrontDoor when
requested content is smaller than 1 byte or larger than 1 MB.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>queryParameters</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>QueryParameters: query parameters to include or exclude (comma separated).</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>queryStringCachingBehavior</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.CacheConfiguration_QueryStringCachingBehavior">
CacheConfiguration_QueryStringCachingBehavior
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>QueryStringCachingBehavior: Defines how Frontdoor caches requests that include query strings. You can ignore any query
strings when caching, ignore specific query strings, cache every request with a unique URL, or cache specific query
strings.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isCompressionEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.CacheConfiguration_IsCompressionEnabled_ARM">
CacheConfiguration_IsCompressionEnabled_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsCompressionEnabled: Indicates whether content compression is enabled. If compression is enabled, content will be
served as compressed if user requests for a compressed version. Content won&rsquo;t be compressed on AzureFrontDoor when
requested content is smaller than 1 byte or larger than 1 MB.</p>
</td>

<em>
string

CacheConfiguration_QueryStringCachingBehavior_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>QueryStringCachingBehavior: Defines how Frontdoor caches requests that include query strings. You can ignore any query
strings when caching, ignore specific query strings, cache every request with a unique URL, or cache specific query
strings.</p>
</td>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOrigin">DeepCreatedOrigin
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profiles_Endpoint_Spec">Profiles_Endpoint_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The main origin of CDN content which is added when creating a CDN endpoint.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Enabled: Origin is enabled for load balancing or not. By default, origin is always enabled.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>hostName</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HostName: The address of the origin. It can be a domain name, IPv4 address, or IPv6 address. This should be unique
across all origins in an endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>httpPort</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HttpPort: The value of the HTTP port. Must be between 1 and 65535.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>httpsPort</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HttpsPort: The value of the HTTPS port. Must be between 1 and 65535.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Origin name which must be unique within the endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originHostHeader</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginHostHeader: The host header value sent to the origin with each request. If you leave this blank, the request
hostname determines this value. Azure CDN origins, such as Web Apps, Blob Storage, and Cloud Services require this host
header value to match the origin hostname by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>priority</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Priority: Priority of origin in given origin group for load balancing. Higher priorities will not be used for load
balancing if any lower priority origin is healthy.Must be between 1 and 5.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkAlias</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkAlias: The Alias of the Private Link resource. Populating this optional field indicates that this origin is
&lsquo;Private&rsquo;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkApprovalMessage</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkApprovalMessage: A custom message to be included in the approval request to connect to the Private Link.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkLocationReference</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#ResourceReference">
genruntime.ResourceReference
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkLocationReference: The location of the Private Link resource. Required only if &lsquo;privateLinkResourceId&rsquo; is
populated</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkResourceReference</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#ResourceReference">
genruntime.ResourceReference
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkResourceReference: The Resource Id of the Private Link resource. Populating this optional field indicates
that this backend is &lsquo;Private&rsquo;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>weight</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Weight: Weight of the origin in given origin group for load balancing. Must be between 1 and 1000</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOriginGroup">DeepCreatedOriginGroup
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profiles_Endpoint_Spec">Profiles_Endpoint_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The origin group for CDN content which is added when creating a CDN endpoint. Traffic is sent to the origins within the
origin group based on origin health.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>healthProbeSettings</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.HealthProbeParameters">
HealthProbeParameters
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HealthProbeSettings: Health probe settings to the origin that is used to determine the health of the origin.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Origin group name which must be unique within the endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>origins</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.ResourceReference">
[]ResourceReference
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Origins: The source of the content being delivered via CDN within given origin group.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>responseBasedOriginErrorDetectionSettings</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.ResponseBasedOriginErrorDetectionParameters">
ResponseBasedOriginErrorDetectionParameters
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ResponseBasedOriginErrorDetectionSettings: The JSON object that contains the properties to determine origin health using
real requests/responses.This property is currently not supported.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>trafficRestorationTimeToHealedOrNewEndpointsInMinutes</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>TrafficRestorationTimeToHealedOrNewEndpointsInMinutes: Time in minutes to shift the traffic to the endpoint gradually
when an unhealthy endpoint comes healthy or a new endpoint is added. Default is 10 mins. This property is currently not
supported.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOriginProperties_ARM">DeepCreatedOriginProperties_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOrigin_ARM">DeepCreatedOrigin_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Properties of the origin created on the CDN endpoint.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Enabled: Origin is enabled for load balancing or not. By default, origin is always enabled.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>hostName</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HostName: The address of the origin. It can be a domain name, IPv4 address, or IPv6 address. This should be unique
across all origins in an endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>httpPort</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HttpPort: The value of the HTTP port. Must be between 1 and 65535.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>httpsPort</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HttpsPort: The value of the HTTPS port. Must be between 1 and 65535.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originHostHeader</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginHostHeader: The host header value sent to the origin with each request. If you leave this blank, the request
hostname determines this value. Azure CDN origins, such as Web Apps, Blob Storage, and Cloud Services require this host
header value to match the origin hostname by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>priority</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Priority: Priority of origin in given origin group for load balancing. Higher priorities will not be used for load
balancing if any lower priority origin is healthy.Must be between 1 and 5.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkAlias</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkAlias: The Alias of the Private Link resource. Populating this optional field indicates that this origin is
&lsquo;Private&rsquo;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkApprovalMessage</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrivateLinkApprovalMessage: A custom message to be included in the approval request to connect to the Private Link.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkLocation</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>privateLinkResourceId</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>weight</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Weight: Weight of the origin in given origin group for load balancing. Must be between 1 and 1000</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRule">DeliveryRule
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy">EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>A rule that specifies a set of actions and conditions</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>actions</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRuleAction">
[]DeliveryRuleAction
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Actions: A list of actions that are executed when all the conditions of a rule are satisfied.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>conditions</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRuleCondition">
[]DeliveryRuleCondition
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Conditions: A list of conditions that must be matched for the actions to be executed</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Name of the rule</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>order</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Order: The order in which the rules are applied for the endpoint. Possible values {0,1,2,3,………}. A rule with a
lesser order will be applied before a rule with a greater order. Rule with order 0 is a special rule. It does not
require any condition and actions listed in it will always be applied.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRule_ARM">DeliveryRule_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_ARM">EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>A rule that specifies a set of actions and conditions</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>actions</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRuleAction_ARM">
[]DeliveryRuleAction_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Actions: A list of actions that are executed when all the conditions of a rule are satisfied.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>conditions</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeliveryRuleCondition_ARM">
[]DeliveryRuleCondition_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Conditions: A list of conditions that must be matched for the actions to be executed</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Name of the rule</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>order</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Order: The order in which the rules are applied for the endpoint. Possible values {0,1,2,3,………}. A rule with a
lesser order will be applied before a rule with a greater order. Rule with order 0 is a special rule. It does not
require any condition and actions listed in it will always be applied.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_ARM">EndpointProperties_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profiles_Endpoint_Spec_ARM">Profiles_Endpoint_Spec_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The JSON object that contains the properties required to create an endpoint.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>contentTypesToCompress</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ContentTypesToCompress: List of content types on which compression applies. The value should be a valid MIME type.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>defaultOriginGroup</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.ResourceReference_ARM">
ResourceReference_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DefaultOriginGroup: A reference to the origin group.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>deliveryPolicy</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_ARM">
EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DeliveryPolicy: A policy that specifies the delivery rules to be used for an endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>geoFilters</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.GeoFilter_ARM">
[]GeoFilter_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>GeoFilters: List of rules defining the user&rsquo;s geo access within a CDN endpoint. Each geo filter defines an access rule
to a specified path or content, e.g. block APAC for path /pictures/</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isCompressionEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsCompressionEnabled: Indicates whether content compression is enabled on CDN. Default value is false. If compression is
enabled, content will be served as compressed if user requests for a compressed version. Content won&rsquo;t be compressed on
CDN when requested content is smaller than 1 byte or larger than 1 MB.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHttpAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsHttpAllowed: Indicates whether HTTP traffic is allowed on the endpoint. Default value is true. At least one protocol
(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHttpsAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsHttpsAllowed: Indicates whether HTTPS traffic is allowed on the endpoint. Default value is true. At least one protocol
(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>optimizationType</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.OptimizationType_ARM">
OptimizationType_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OptimizationType: Specifies what scenario the customer wants this CDN endpoint to optimize for, e.g. Download, Media
services. With this information, CDN can apply scenario driven optimization.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originGroups</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOriginGroup_ARM">
[]DeepCreatedOriginGroup_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginGroups: The origin groups comprising of origins that are used for load balancing the traffic based on availability.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originHostHeader</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginHostHeader: The host header value sent to the origin with each request. This property at Endpoint is only allowed
when endpoint uses single origin and can be overridden by the same property specified at origin.If you leave this blank,
the request hostname determines this value. Azure CDN origins, such as Web Apps, Blob Storage, and Cloud Services
require this host header value to match the origin hostname by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originPath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginPath: A directory path on the origin that CDN can use to retrieve content from, e.g.
contoso.cloudapp.net/originpath.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>origins</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOrigin_ARM">
[]DeepCreatedOrigin_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Origins: The source of the content being delivered via CDN.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>probePath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ProbePath: Path to a file hosted on the origin which helps accelerate delivery of the dynamic content and calculate the
most optimal routes for the CDN. This is relative to the origin path. This property is only relevant when using a single
origin.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>queryStringCachingBehavior</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.QueryStringCachingBehavior_ARM">
QueryStringCachingBehavior_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>QueryStringCachingBehavior: Defines how CDN caches requests that include query strings. You can ignore any query strings
when caching, bypass caching to prevent requests that contain query strings from being cached, or cache every request
with a unique URL.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>urlSigningKeys</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlSigningKey_ARM">
[]UrlSigningKey_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>UrlSigningKeys: List of keys used to validate the signed URL hashes.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>webApplicationFirewallPolicyLink</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_WebApplicationFirewallPolicyLink_ARM">
EndpointProperties_WebApplicationFirewallPolicyLink_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>WebApplicationFirewallPolicyLink: Defines the Web Application Firewall policy for the endpoint (if applicable)</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_STATUS_ARM">EndpointProperties_STATUS_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profiles_Endpoint_STATUS_ARM">Profiles_Endpoint_STATUS_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The JSON object that contains the properties required to create an endpoint.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>contentTypesToCompress</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ContentTypesToCompress: List of content types on which compression applies. The value should be a valid MIME type.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customDomains</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedCustomDomain_STATUS_ARM">
[]DeepCreatedCustomDomain_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomDomains: The custom domains under the endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>defaultOriginGroup</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.ResourceReference_STATUS_ARM">
ResourceReference_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DefaultOriginGroup: A reference to the origin group.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>deliveryPolicy</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_STATUS_ARM">
EndpointProperties_DeliveryPolicy_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DeliveryPolicy: A policy that specifies the delivery rules to be used for an endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>geoFilters</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.GeoFilter_STATUS_ARM">
[]GeoFilter_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>GeoFilters: List of rules defining the user&rsquo;s geo access within a CDN endpoint. Each geo filter defines an access rule
to a specified path or content, e.g. block APAC for path /pictures/</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>hostName</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HostName: The host name of the endpoint structured as {endpointName}.{DNSZone}, e.g. contoso.azureedge.net</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isCompressionEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsCompressionEnabled: Indicates whether content compression is enabled on CDN. Default value is false. If compression is
enabled, content will be served as compressed if user requests for a compressed version. Content won&rsquo;t be compressed on
CDN when requested content is smaller than 1 byte or larger than 1 MB.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHttpAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsHttpAllowed: Indicates whether HTTP traffic is allowed on the endpoint. Default value is true. At least one protocol
(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHttpsAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsHttpsAllowed: Indicates whether HTTPS traffic is allowed on the endpoint. Default value is true. At least one protocol
(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>optimizationType</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.OptimizationType_STATUS_ARM">
OptimizationType_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OptimizationType: Specifies what scenario the customer wants this CDN endpoint to optimize for, e.g. Download, Media
services. With this information, CDN can apply scenario driven optimization.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originGroups</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOriginGroup_STATUS_ARM">
[]DeepCreatedOriginGroup_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginGroups: The origin groups comprising of origins that are used for load balancing the traffic based on availability.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originHostHeader</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginHostHeader: The host header value sent to the origin with each request. This property at Endpoint is only allowed
when endpoint uses single origin and can be overridden by the same property specified at origin.If you leave this blank,
the request hostname determines this value. Azure CDN origins, such as Web Apps, Blob Storage, and Cloud Services
require this host header value to match the origin hostname by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originPath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginPath: A directory path on the origin that CDN can use to retrieve content from, e.g.
contoso.cloudapp.net/originpath.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>origins</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.DeepCreatedOrigin_STATUS_ARM">
[]DeepCreatedOrigin_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Origins: The source of the content being delivered via CDN.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>probePath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ProbePath: Path to a file hosted on the origin which helps accelerate delivery of the dynamic content and calculate the
most optimal routes for the CDN. This is relative to the origin path. This property is only relevant when using a single
origin.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>provisioningState</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.EndpointProperties_ProvisioningState_STATUS_ARM">
EndpointProperties_ProvisioningState_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ProvisioningState: Provisioning status of the endpoint.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>queryStringCachingBehavior</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.QueryStringCachingBehavior_STATUS_ARM">
QueryStringCachingBehavior_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>QueryStringCachingBehavior: Defines how CDN caches requests that include query strings. You can ignore any query strings
when caching, bypass caching to prevent requests that contain query strings from being cached, or cache every request
with a unique URL.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>GeoFilters: List of rules defining the user&rsquo;s geo access within a CDN endpoint. Each geo filter defines an access rule
to a specified path or content, e.g. block APAC for path /pictures/</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isCompressionEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsCompressionEnabled: Indicates whether content compression is enabled on CDN. Default value is false. If compression is
enabled, content will be served as compressed if user requests for a compressed version. Content won&rsquo;t be compressed on
CDN when requested content is smaller than 1 byte or larger than 1 MB.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHttpAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>

<td>
<code>isHttpsAllowed</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

(HTTP or HTTPS) must be allowed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>location</code><br/>

OptimizationType
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>

services. With this information, CDN can apply scenario driven optimization.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originGroups</code><br/>

[]DeepCreatedOriginGroup
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginGroups: The origin groups comprising of origins that are used for load balancing the traffic based on availability.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originHostHeader</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OriginHostHeader: The host header value sent to the origin with each request. This property at Endpoint is only allowed
when endpoint uses single origin and can be overridden by the same property specified at origin.If you leave this blank,
the request hostname determines this value. Azure CDN origins, such as Web Apps, Blob Storage, and Cloud Services
require this host header value to match the origin hostname by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>originPath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>

contoso.cloudapp.net/originpath.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>

[]DeepCreatedOrigin
</a>

<td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>owner</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#KnownResourceReference">
genruntime.KnownResourceReference
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Owner: The owner of the resource. The owner controls where the resource goes when it is deployed. The owner also
controls the resources lifecycle. When the owner is deleted the resource will also be deleted. Owner is expected to be a
reference to a cdn.azure.com/Profile resource</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>probePath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ProbePath: Path to a file hosted on the origin which helps accelerate delivery of the dynamic content and calculate the
most optimal routes for the CDN. This is relative to the origin path. This property is only relevant when using a single
origin.</p>
</td>
</tr>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.QueryStringCachingBehavior">QueryStringCachingBehavior
(<code>string</code> alias)</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profiles_Endpoint_Spec">Profiles_Endpoint_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Defines how CDN caches requests that include query strings. You can ignore any query strings when caching, bypass
caching to prevent requests that contain query strings from being cached, or cache every request with a unique URL.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Value</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr><td><p>&#34;BypassCaching&#34;</p></td>
<td></td>
</tr><tr><td><p>&#34;IgnoreQueryString&#34;</p></td>
<td></td>
</tr><tr><td><p>&#34;NotSet&#34;</p></td>
<td></td>
</tr><tr><td><p>&#34;UseQueryString&#34;</p></td>
<td></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Sku">Sku
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profile_Spec">Profile_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Standard_Verizon = The SKU name for a Standard Verizon CDN profile.
Premium_Verizon = The SKU name for a Premium Verizon
CDN profile.
Custom_Verizon = The SKU name for a Custom Verizon CDN profile.
Standard_Akamai = The SKU name for an
Akamai CDN profile.
Standard_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile for VOD, Web and download scenarios using
GB based billing model.
Standard_Microsoft = The SKU name for a Standard Microsoft CDN profile.
Standard_AzureFrontDoor
=  The SKU name for an Azure Front Door Standard profile.
Premium_AzureFrontDoor = The SKU name for an Azure Front Door
Premium profile.
Standard_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile for VOD, Web and download
scenarios using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing model.
Standard_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile
for VOD, Web and download scenarios using monthly average peak bandwidth billing model.
StandardPlus_ChinaCdn = The SKU
name for a China CDN profile for live-streaming using GB based billing model.
StandardPlus_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The
SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing
model.
StandardPlus_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using monthly average
peak bandwidth billing model.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Sku_Name">
Sku_Name
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Name of the pricing tier.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Sku_ARM">Sku_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profile_Spec_ARM">Profile_Spec_ARM</a>)
</p>

Premium_Verizon = The SKU name for a Premium Verizon

GB based billing model.
Standard_Microsoft = The SKU name for a Standard Microsoft CDN profile.
Standard_AzureFrontDoor
=  The SKU name for an Azure Front Door Standard profile.
Premium_AzureFrontDoor = The SKU name for an Azure Front Door
Premium profile.
Standard_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile for VOD, Web and download
scenarios using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing model.
Standard_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile
for VOD, Web and download scenarios using monthly average peak bandwidth billing model.
StandardPlus_ChinaCdn = The SKU
name for a China CDN profile for live-streaming using GB based billing model.
StandardPlus_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The
SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing
model.
StandardPlus_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using monthly average
peak bandwidth billing model.</p>

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Sku_STATUS">Sku_STATUS
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Profile_STATUS">Profile_STATUS</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Standard_Verizon = The SKU name for a Standard Verizon CDN profile.
Premium_Verizon = The SKU name for a Premium Verizon
CDN profile.
Custom_Verizon = The SKU name for a Custom Verizon CDN profile.
Standard_Akamai = The SKU name for an
Akamai CDN profile.
Standard_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile for VOD, Web and download scenarios using
GB based billing model.
Standard_Microsoft = The SKU name for a Standard Microsoft CDN profile.
Standard_AzureFrontDoor
=  The SKU name for an Azure Front Door Standard profile.
Premium_AzureFrontDoor = The SKU name for an Azure Front Door
Premium profile.
Standard_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile for VOD, Web and download
scenarios using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing model.
Standard_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN profile
for VOD, Web and download scenarios using monthly average peak bandwidth billing model.
StandardPlus_ChinaCdn = The SKU
name for a China CDN profile for live-streaming using GB based billing model.
StandardPlus_955BandWidth_ChinaCdn = The
SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using 95-5 peak bandwidth billing
model.
StandardPlus_AvgBandWidth_ChinaCdn = The SKU name for a China CDN live-streaming profile using monthly average
peak bandwidth billing model.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>name</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.Sku_Name_STATUS">
Sku_Name_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Name: Name of the pricing tier.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters">UrlRedirectActionParameters
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectAction">UrlRedirectAction</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Defines the parameters for the url redirect action.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customFragment</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomFragment: Fragment to add to the redirect URL. Fragment is the part of the URL that comes after #. Do not include
the #.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customHostname</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomHostname: Host to redirect. Leave empty to use the incoming host as the destination host.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customPath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomPath: The full path to redirect. Path cannot be empty and must start with /. Leave empty to use the incoming path
as destination path.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customQueryString</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomQueryString: The set of query strings to be placed in the redirect URL. Setting this value would replace any
existing query string; leave empty to preserve the incoming query string. Query string must be in <key>=<value> format.
? and &amp; will be added automatically so do not include them.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>destinationProtocol</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_DestinationProtocol">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_DestinationProtocol
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DestinationProtocol: Protocol to use for the redirect. The default value is MatchRequest</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>redirectType</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RedirectType: The redirect type the rule will use when redirecting traffic.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>typeName</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_TypeName">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_TypeName
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType_STATUS">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RedirectType: The redirect type the rule will use when redirecting traffic.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>typeName</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_TypeName_STATUS">

<h3 id="cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_STATUS_ARM">UrlRedirectActionParameters_STATUS_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectAction_STATUS_ARM">UrlRedirectAction_STATUS_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Defines the parameters for the url redirect action.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customFragment</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomFragment: Fragment to add to the redirect URL. Fragment is the part of the URL that comes after #. Do not include
the #.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customHostname</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomHostname: Host to redirect. Leave empty to use the incoming host as the destination host.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customPath</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomPath: The full path to redirect. Path cannot be empty and must start with /. Leave empty to use the incoming path
as destination path.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customQueryString</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomQueryString: The set of query strings to be placed in the redirect URL. Setting this value would replace any
existing query string; leave empty to preserve the incoming query string. Query string must be in <key>=<value> format.
? and &amp; will be added automatically so do not include them.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>destinationProtocol</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_DestinationProtocol_STATUS_ARM">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_DestinationProtocol_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DestinationProtocol: Protocol to use for the redirect. The default value is MatchRequest</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>redirectType</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType_STATUS_ARM">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_RedirectType_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RedirectType: The redirect type the rule will use when redirecting traffic.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>typeName</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#cdn.azure.com/v1api20210601.UrlRedirectActionParameters_TypeName_STATUS_ARM">
UrlRedirectActionParameters_TypeName_STATUS_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<em>

</em>

</td>
</tr>

<td>
<code>preserveUnmatchedPath</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

</td>
</tr>

<td>
<code>sourcePattern</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>

blank, all strings are matched.</p>
</td>
